# VE-01 (obs 395) — M vs R divergence: where the read lands outside the lexical range

> Read-only. Generated 2026-06-11. **M** = mechanical term-gloss (lexical range). **R** = verse-specific read sense. Compared for **3702** term-in-verses that have BOTH. Crude 5-char-stem overlap; threshold 0.25. **Material divergence: 1439** (277 ZERO-overlap, 1162 LOW). This NAVIGATES to candidates — it does NOT validate. Read the verse + both values before judging (metaphor / extended sense / homonym / too-narrow gloss / read error all live here).
